A Stroll Through the Market: Onlookers 119

The Gold and Silver Market is Beneficial Without Being Wasteful; Gold Bonds Start to Play a Role; a Turning Point in the Stock Market's Future

For the past twelve years, gold and silver trading has almost never completely stopped for even a day. Therefore, the opening of the gold and silver market today only indicates: (1) the black market becomes the open market; (2) the illegal becomes legal; (3) the scattered and unorganized becomes centralized and organized.

These three meanings can be said to be the unified spirit of all the recent measures taken by the financial authorities, and can also be said to be very Confucian and Mencian.

Ran Qiu asked Confucius, "What is 'beneficial without being wasteful'?"

Confucius said, "To benefit the people according to what they find beneficial, is that not beneficial without being wasteful?"

That is to say, if the people think something is beneficial, the government should allow them to do it. If the people benefit, the government also benefits. Isn't that beneficial without being wasteful?

The current financial authorities have deeply grasped the essence of Confucianism. Underground money houses and black market interest rates are what people find beneficial, so the government opens them up. Gold and currency transactions are busy in the black market, which is what the people find beneficial, so the government opens them up. All such things are the implementation of Confucian and Mencian philosophy, and who can say it is not appropriate!

Gold and silver trading has gone from illegal to legal, and from scattered to centralized. From now on, there will be a bright future.

To what extent will this future be? First of all, it must be understood that all three hundred and sixty industries are trending towards an equilibrium of profits. From this point of view, the future progress and retreat of the gold and silver market is most likely to save the stock market.

The stock market in the past week can be said to have had bad luck. From today onwards, it will be easy to support each other and sing in harmony.

Some say: In the past, there have been markets such as cloth, so the stock market is not alone. However, when actual sales are smooth, cloth does have the function of assisting the stock market. The situation has changed slightly in the past week, and the capital required for cloth is also large, while gold and silver transactions use one tael as a unit, which is easy and convenient. Therefore, it is much more convenient to carry the stock market than with cloth, etc.

The most readily available thing for the gold and silver market and the stock market to support each other is gold bonds.

Gold bonds have been listed for sale until today, and have been in a state of decline. From now on, the daily hedging of gold bonds may be realized.

The authorities may have two thoughts about the daily hedging of gold bonds: (1) Sales are effective; (2) Controlling the gold and silver market also has a handle.

If you don't believe it, let's look at the new changes in the next week or two: (1) Gold bonds may replace the deflated foreign exchange transfer certificates as a tool for buying and selling. (2) The five jiao daily interest rate base may produce a "formula" market interest rate in the daily hedging of gold bonds to adjust the situation.

There is no need to say more to those with discerning eyes.

Now, what ordinary people are concerned about is what role will the opening of the gold and silver market have on prices and the value of silver dollars? First of all, of course, is that the tide will rise with the boat. Secondly, the price of silver dollars on the street will not diverge too much. Gold Bonds Start to Play a Role; a Turning Point in the Stock Market's Future

Discount Committee Stipulations: Supplementary Measures for Industrial Loans 123

(2) Those whose original loans have expired and both principal and interest have been paid off may apply for loans again, and the original review standards shall still be used for separate review and actual lending.

Mei Wu Shows Off His Skills

At ten minutes, Jialing suddenly shot hard, and Liang De saved the danger, but he continued to lose two corner kicks. Once, Zhu Zai headed the ball high on the left. Once, Li Dahui suddenly entered the center and angrily shot from 25 yards, but it was blocked by An Dachen into a corner kick. At about 15 minutes, Wu Lun crossed the ball, and Hou Lu rushed in for a shot, but Wu Lun was offside first, so it couldn't be counted. Jialing suddenly went to the left wing position, dribbled the ball straight up, and crossed it horizontally near the baseline. When the ball crossed in front of the goal, Siweia was there to receive it and quickly passed it to the front of the goal. At that time, Mei Wu changed to the central open position, and the ball just happened to arrive, so he shot into the goal from close range, scoring the first point.

After Wah Luen lost this goal, they immediately switched Chunfa and Zhu Yongqiang's positions. Not long after, Dahui had a chance to shoot, but it was again blocked by An Dachen into a corner kick. The ball came to Wenzhi, who ordered Chunfa to shoot, but it became a high-angle shot. At 36 minutes, Mei Wu dribbled the ball deep, and Hou Rongsheng tried hard to resist, already entangled near the baseline. At that time, Rongsheng originally wanted to kick the ball against Mei Wu's foot to make it bounce out of bounds for a goal kick, but although the ball hit Mei Wu, it rolled diagonally without crossing the boundary. Mei Wu took the opportunity to raise his foot and swipe it horizontally, and it was as if he had divine help. The ball he shot flew diagonally into the Wah Luen goal. The ball flew into the net diagonally along the right post. Because of the oblique angle and the speed of its arrival, Liang De was unable to save it. Wah Luen lost the second goal.

Wah Luen Changes Formation

Seeing that the defense had weaknesses, Wah Luen urgently changed Xie Jinhong to the central defender, Miao Zai to the east left back, and Zhang Jinhai to the front line to lead the attack. Li Chunfa changed to the left center back. However, because the trend had already been established, there was no way to reverse the defeat for a while. At 42 minutes, in the course of Si Lu's intrusion into the hinterland, Xie Jinhong and Hou Rongsheng cooperated to entangle him, joining forces to sandwich him in the center, so that they rolled into a ball and fell to the ground together. The referee then awarded Wah Luen a penalty kick. The ball was kicked by Wu Lun, but because he kicked it too off to the side, it only hit the right post of the goal and did not go in. So in the first half, Wah Luen only lost two goals, which was considered a blessing in disguise.

When the second half started again, the Western lineup remained the same. Wah Luen's new lineup was as follows:

Yu Yaode Miao Changrong Hou Rongsheng Liu Songsheng Xie Jinhong Li Chunfa Li Dahui Zou Wenzhi Zhang Jinhai Feng Jingxiang Zhu Yongqiang

At this time, Wah Luen adjusted its lineup, which was obviously better than the first half. But after only two minutes of the game, Li Dahui angrily shot into the goal. When An Dachen held the ball, Zhang Jinhai had already rushed to him. An Dachen was afraid of losing the ball, so he patted the ball to avoid it, but Zhang also chased after him, blocking him in front and preventing him from kicking the ball out. Qi Liqi saw this and suddenly burst into anger, rushing behind Zhang and hitting him hard. Although Zhang fell to the ground, the penalty kick had been awarded. This ball was still taken by the "Desperate Saburo," who executed it with one stroke of the knife, and Wah Luen regained a 2-1 situation.

Reversal Missed

Since they had regained a taste of sweetness, Wah Luen's prestige was even more dazzling. Once, Zhu Yongqiang crossed the ball, and the Wah Luen troops advanced towards the goal, but it was finally pushed out by An Dachen. However, Wah Luen's prestige was too great at that time, and at 15 minutes, Feng Jingxiang made a wonderful shot and scored a goal, making it a 2-2 tie. For a moment, the spectators cheered, thinking that Wah Luen had this, then victory was expected.

Unexpectedly, three minutes later, Siweia had a chance on the periphery and angrily scored a goal. Although Miao Changrong tried hard to entangle him by running, he was unable to get the position and was still cut in for a shot. The ball was very fast, and although Liang De reached out to touch the ball, it still slid into the net, so Western took the lead again. After that, Zhang Jinhai injured his foot and lost his ability to charge at the goal, so Wah Luen was unable to win again. There were still two things worth recording after that. One was that the football exploded at 31 minutes, and the other was that Hou Ziyuan came out to cross the ball. Although Zhang Jinhai was injured in the foot, he still struggled to rush up, threatening An Dachen so that he could only leave the goal and rush forward, hurriedly pushing the ball out. The ball was obtained by Feng Ershu, who immediately lobbed an empty goal. Unfortunately, the momentum was slightly poor and it did not fall directly into the goal but fell on the top of the net. Otherwise, this could have been a chance to reverse the defeat, because if the game was extended, Wah Luen might not have been able to finally beat the drum of victory, which is a pity.

Hong Kong Chinese League Painfully Loses Governor's Cup: Feng Jingxiang Unmatched Among Peers; Xiao Miao Unstable; Da Hui Out of Form 137

[Hong Kong 21st Dispatch] In this year's Governor's Cup, the Western League team of the Football Association unjustly defeated several Chinese players yesterday due to their inexplicable performance. Although the Chinese team has already secured the finals for this season's Special Silver Shield, and the league championship and runner-up awards are practically guaranteed for Chinese players, and the Memorial Cup is expected to be ours, the fact that the Chinese League team, with such talented players, lost the Governor's Cup is more than just a minor imperfection. Having suffered a humiliating 6-1 defeat the first time, losing the final match again yesterday can be considered a great disgrace.

Considering our lineup yesterday, we had eight national team players, which is already a formidable organization in Hong Kong. Furthermore, comparing each player individually or assessing the entire team's skills, the opposing team was no match for our heroes. Therefore, we had no reason to lose our prestige. However, after 23 minutes of the game, Chia-neng suddenly showed off his cleverness, dribbling up from the left wing position, disrupting the steps of our defenders and allowing him to calmly pass the ball across the goal, ultimately allowing Meigo, who had moved to the center, to score first. Then, in the 36th minute of the first half, Hou Zi, who is usually so adept at making swift clearances, acted like an old woman trying to act young, fumbling with fancy moves on the baseline while facing the extremely threatening Meigo. As a result, he lost another goal in that person's miraculous shot. Afterwards, although the generals exerted themselves in the second half and managed to tie the score 2-2 within 15 minutes, Miao Changrong ultimately lacked experience. At that time, Silva gained possession and advanced quickly, and Xiao Miao was fiercely chasing and pressing, holding the line. However, because he didn't position himself correctly, Silva managed to flick the ball in, miraculously scoring again. Thus, the opponents leisurely accepted the Governor's Cup from the hands of Governor Sir Alexander Grantham, their faces beaming with joy. This is truly something that makes Chinese fans feel suffocated.

Association Chinese League:

Xie Jinhong (South China), Yu Yaode (South China), Hou Zhasheng (South China), Liu Songsheng (South China), Miao Changrong (Chinese), Zhang Jinhai (South China), Li Dahui (Bus), Zou Wenzhi (Bus), Zhu Yongqiang (South China), Li Chunfa (Bus), Feng Jingxiang (South China)

Association Western League:

Dosha (Navy), Anderson (Army), Luo Cha (Joseph), Qi Liqi (Army), Li Annar (Joseph), Luo Bianchen (Army), Meigo (Hong Kong), Chia-neng (Hong Kong), Hou Lu (Police), Wu Lun (Hong Kong), Silva (Joseph)

Miao Changrong is a rising young player with little experience in big games, so it's not surprising that he didn't perform up to par in such an occasion. The most surprising thing is that the two best center backs in Hong Kong, who were as lively as dragons and tigers after the game against Eastern the other day, were completely out of form yesterday. Xie Jinhong, returning to the left back position this time, couldn't find the same form as he usually has as the center back for South China. The most unfortunate thing is that Li Dahui was too out of form, not only completely lacking the ability to cut in and shoot, but also his powerful crosses were not up to par. I believe it's because he usually plays too much small-sided football. I always say that small-sided football can only be used as an introductory path to practicing big football. Once you play well in the big football circle, you shouldn't engage in small-sided football anymore, otherwise it will be more harmful than beneficial. The reason is that small-sided football and big football have different weights, the fields are different sizes, and the force used when kicking is different. Big football players being distracted by small-sided football will lead to the degradation of big football skills. Considering the "almost there but not quite" nature of Dahui's crosses yesterday, I dare to assert that he is harming himself by playing too much small-sided football.

My frank words are naturally a way of holding the virtuous accountable, which stems from deep love and unintentional bluntness. Looking at the bigger picture, although the Chinese League unfortunately lost, the fighting spirit in the second half and the quick wit to change the lineup when things seemed unfavorable are worthy of praise. The old Feng Jingxiang is still strong and plays with great skill, not only scoring the tying goal but also fighting bravely, which is truly admirable. Honestly speaking, Zhang Jinhai's center back play is good, but he is ultimately better as a striker than a center back. If he hadn't injured his foot after switching to center forward yesterday, I believe he would have turned the tide with his sprinting ability. In the second half, the entire national team forward line was brought on, but they still couldn't salvage the defeat. What else can be said?

Objectively speaking, yesterday's game wasn't that the opponents played well, but that we played badly. The loss was too undeserved. However, I must specially point out and praise some of the opponent's key players. Li Annar, the center back, knows the Chinese style of play well, and he himself is brave and physically imposing, making him a strong opponent for our Chinese team. Chia-neng is undoubtedly the best left winger in Hong Kong. The most unexpected thing was the agility of Hong Kong Club's Meigo, which was truly beyond our expectations. Although both of his goals seemed to have an element of luck, his ability to succeed in luck was due to his daring and willingness to act, and not easily letting go of good opportunities. Also, the sudden improvement in the performance of the two Portuguese players, Silva and Luo Cha, is worthy of praise. They also have their own way of deserving victory.

Free Talk

Knife Fish Noodles 138

— Chen Yixian

Feng Xuan, as a retainer in Lord Mengchang's household, sang loudly, "Let's go home with my long sword!" The first verse was about the lack of fish in the diet. The second course of a Western meal is always fish, and sophisticated diners even have silver knives for eating fish. It can be seen that whether Chinese or foreigners, fish is always a necessary part of a meal. Now that the peach blossoms are beginning to bloom, knife fish are on the market, and I will talk a little about knife fish noodles.

Knife fish is the earliest fish of the year, with the freshest taste and the most bones, so ordinary families do not prepare this dish. Last February, I went to Yangzhou on business and passed through Zhenjiang, where a friend invited me to morning tea. People in the Yangzhou and Zhenjiang area start their breakfast with a pot of tea, followed by wine, braised pork, dried bean curd threads, and then steamed buns, dumplings, and noodles. Braised pork is eaten with vinegar-soaked ginger shreds, which is naturally a specialty of Zhenjiang, but their knife fish noodles are unique to this area. The host specifically instructed the waiter to make them "thin noodles with ample soup." When the noodles arrived, there was a bowl of thick soup, and only after eating halfway did I see a small amount of noodles, which tasted extremely fresh and had no fish bones. My friend said that knife fish noodles must be eaten in February, because even though this fish is still available in the market before Qingming in March, it is no longer valued.

Chicken, duck, pork, and beef are available all year round, but fish have their seasons. For example, knife fish are available when peach blossoms bloom, pufferfish when willow catkins are in the air, tu fu fish (also known as yellow croaker) when rapeseed flowers bloom, shad during the beginning of summer, yellow eel is best in early summer, and its taste and quality deteriorate after the Summer Solstice, while perch is best during frost descent. Each fish has its unique beauty, such as the liver of perch, the belly of shad, the head of catfish, the tongue of crucian carp and a piece of the back under the head, the flower of mandarin fish, the fin of pomfret, and the swimming bladder and white flesh in the belly of grass carp, which only gourmets can appreciate.

The Tragedy of the Middle Ground 139

— Xiao Feng

In this day and age, it's really not easy to speak. If you lean too far to the left, you'll be labeled a "communist bandit," and if you lean too far to the right, you'll be labeled "stubborn" and "reactionary." Perhaps being a non-leftist, non-rightist centrist should allow you to please both sides. However, that's not the case. If you're not careful, you'll be criticized for being "opportunistic" or "sycophantic."

Having read the three articles recently published by Mr. Liang Shuming, he presents himself as an impartial peacemaker, holding the Nationalist Party fully responsible for the war while also demanding that "the Communist Party should announce that the three years of fighting were a last resort, and express deep remorse for the damage caused to the country and the people." Although it's a bit contradictory, it's necessary to appear as an "impartial person outside the Nationalists and Communists." Unfortunately, Mr. Liang's masterpiece didn't win applause, but rather drew jeers. Several publications on the left, such as "Zhongjian" and "Xin Shidai," launched a siege with titles like "Questioning Liang Shuming," "Reprimanding Liang Shuming," and "Liang Shuming's Political Illusions." The publication on the right, "Xin Xiwang," also expressed opposition, arguing that "it seems as if this war was entirely a one-man show by the Nationalist Party, and the Communist Party didn't even climb onto the stage, which is difficult to accept." They unanimously considered Mr. Liang's invented "posthumous conferment method" to be a very ridiculous approach. Even Mr. Liang, who is skilled at observing the situation and trying to please everyone, couldn't avoid being attacked from both sides. No wonder the great liberal master "crossed the river soldier" Hu Shi has remained silent since flying south, truly a wise man who understands the times.

During the Political Consultative Conference, because both the Nationalists and Communists were vying for the support of centrists, small parties and social elites who sought survival in the cracks enjoyed a moment of great popularity, with the pleasure of pleasing both sides. With the changes in the political situation, centrists have either joined Yang Zhu or Mo Di, and are feeling the pain of "it's difficult to please both sides" and "displeasing everyone."

The late Japanese professor Rongjiro Kawai put it well: "We who fight against conservative reactionaries on the right and support oppressed ideas, and who fight against materialistic Marxist ideas on the left, are considered the same as Marxists by the right and the same as conservatives by the left. We may be attacked from both sides, but this is precisely where the unique mission of liberalism lies, and the valuable task that liberalism should undertake." These words truly express the sorrow and anger of a centrist.

Peaceful Resolution 140

— Wang Deyun

I have been working in a law firm for many years, so I have some contact with various lawsuits and case proceedings. I am busy all day writing about defendants and plaintiffs, and life is almost as stereotyped as "in accordance with the above." I don't seem to be very interested in law, but I often pay attention to the clients of various levels who patronize the firm. The clients are quite diverse: workers, merchants, scholars, officials, rickshaw pullers... almost everything is included. They almost always talk to the lawyer with tense faces, anxiously and agitatedly. This impression often makes me think: there are so many disputes between people.

Of course, some cases seem to require resorting to law. But there are also some cases that are not a big deal, and can be resolved peacefully, but people often don't think of this shortcut, and just act emotionally. In fact, the gains from reconciliation are always more satisfactory than the outcome of litigation, which is undeniable. Even lawyers do not hope to litigate, and often mediate from the middle, hoping to resolve the matter and "turn swords into plowshares."

Of course, the more advanced civilization is and the more complex the social environment, the more conflicts and conflicts of interest between people increase, which seems to be inevitable. However, unwise behaviors caused by disputes often lead to both sides being injured and irreparable. Therefore, the best buffer for disputes is to seek a peaceful solution. This is true not only for private individuals and groups, but also, in a broader sense, even for wars between countries and friction and cold wars between nations.

Flyer Company 142

— Mao Yi

In England, there is a company that specializes in distributing flyers on behalf of advertising companies, manufacturers, or other individuals. Large-scale "flyer companies" even have the names and addresses of one hundred million people from all over the world. One of them was founded by Einstein's nephew, who fled to England on the day Hitler seized power, with only a five-pound note in his pocket. Within six years, he became a big boss employing 250 people.

Any client can entrust the flyer company to send their flyers to people they want to reach but whose names and addresses they don't know. Although the flyer company is responsible for delivering the flyers to the designated recipients, they do not disclose the recipients' names and addresses, because names and addresses are their trade secrets. On the other hand, if the flyers are returned by the post office due to unsuccessful delivery, the flyer company will refund the delivery fee to the client proportionally.

The fee for sending flyers depends on the number of flyers and the nature of the recipients. Usually, it costs 48 pounds for every 23,600 copies. A waterproof glass raincoat manufacturer paid 48 pounds, but after only 6,000 flyers were sent out, he excitedly called the flyer company to request that they stop sending them. This is because his inventory was sold out after the first batch of flyers was sent out.

Not long ago, a soap merchant commissioned the flyer company to distribute flyers to 12 million housewives in England, at a cost of two pounds per thousand copies, totaling approximately 24,000 pounds. (Needless to say, postage and paper are the responsibility of the client, but it is also possible to pay the flyer company to handle it.)

The flyers distributed by the flyer company are not limited to commercial purposes. British political parties often use them to distribute political flyers. Once, George Bernard Shaw wanted to draw the attention of every member of the House of Commons, the House of Lords, and the Irish Parliament to his "simplified spelling scheme," so he also entrusted the flyer company to send out his proposal.

How does the flyer company find so many names and addresses? Naturally, telephone books, directories of prominent people, address books, and the like are used. In addition, the company also sends people to read newspapers, recording every name and address that may be used sooner or later. Furthermore, they also purchase lists of participants in various gatherings, extracting useful information.

Once names and addresses are in the hands of the flyer company, they are sorted and classified, becoming their assets. I think if the household registration section of the Shanghai Civil Affairs Bureau were to operate a side business, setting up a flyer company like the one in England would be a good deal.

What Kind of Person is Mrs. Truman? 144

— Baozhu

When it comes to Mrs. Roosevelt, almost everyone knows that she was a very shrewd, capable, and great woman, and a good helper to the former President of the United States. However, Mrs. Truman is the opposite, remaining silent and unknown, even though she has been the First Lady for almost four years. Not to mention that Chinese people don't know her, even Americans themselves don't pay much attention to her. In general, apart from "an ordinary housewife," there is nothing else worth mentioning about her.

However, people who are close to her know that this American First Lady is not as ordinary as people imagine. She was originally Truman's top advisor. During the presidential campaign, President Truman always introduced his wife as "my boss."

Mrs. Truman's name is Bess, and her maiden name is Wallace. She was born in a very wealthy and famous family in Independence, Missouri. After graduating from Independence High School, she attended the famous Barstow School for Girls in Kansas City. Although Bess was a daughter of a wealthy family, she taught at the girls' school. At that time, she had not yet married Truman. This June will mark their 30th wedding anniversary.

Because she is naturally不喜欢交际和出风头, there are fewer opportunities for people to get to know her. In fact, she is not only a good housewife, but also a woman with great insight, talent, and knowledge.

Although she has never given a speech, every one of President Truman's speeches has been carefully read, studied, and corrected by her first. When Mr. Truman first became a senator, Bess worked as his private secretary. Later, because her daughter Margaret was not in good health when she was young, she stopped working to take care of her child and manage the household. She likes to read, especially history and biographies. As the president of such a large country, Truman naturally has little time to read, but it doesn't matter, his wife often reads articles about world events and summarizes them for the president. Bess, like her husband and daughter, also loves music. In addition, she likes to play bridge, but unfortunately she doesn't have much time now.

Mrs. Truman does not photograph well, so the First Lady seen in news photos is short and fat. In fact, this sixty-four-year-old lady is not that ugly. She has a small face, well-proportioned features, blue-gray eyes, and silver-gray hair that is always neatly combed. When she first entered the White House, she often saw newspapers and magazines saying that she looked like a "housekeeper." Once, she said to her friends with a wry smile, "What's wrong with that?" Bess also likes to wear elegant clothes and high-quality fabrics; however, she is very frugal. During the day, she always wears very ordinary clothes, but she is more particular about her evening gowns.

American government officials, senators, and their wives like to attend Mrs. Truman's banquets, because Bess is very kind and amiable, making them feel like they are at home. The seating arrangements do not have to be arranged according to rank. No matter how many guests there are, the First Lady must talk to each one. "She always talks about you, and doesn't brag about herself," one guest told others upon returning. She also cooks very well. During the war, even though she was already the wife of the vice president, she did not have a maid, just like other ordinary American families. She said, "My husband likes to eat steak and fried yams. As long as I make these two dishes for him every night, he is very happy."

Unlike ordinary officials' wives who travel to scenic spots to escape the heat, Bess likes to return to her old home every summer to live with her mother, driving away the guards, digging in the mud in the garden, watering flowers, or inviting her old friends to play bridge.

Mrs. Truman is not exactly great but certainly not stupid or vulgar. She is a meritorious person to her husband, daughter, and family, and naturally, she is not without benefit to the United States.
